        "title": "The Martian Movie and Our Real Journey to Mars",
        "body": "<p><a class=\"tumblr_blog\" href=\"http://nasa.tumblr.com/post/130352836054\">nasa</a>:</p>\n<blockquote>\n<p>The Martian movie is set 20 years in the future, but here at NASA we are already developing many of the technologies that appear in the film. The movie takes the work we’re doing and extends it into fiction set in the 2030s, when NASA astronauts are regularly traveling to Mars and living on the surface. Here are a few ways The Martian movie compares to what we’re really doing on our journey to Mars:</p>\n<p><b>Analog Missions</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/b93f3d9373c5fe5ccdfbd79e7c0d472e/tumblr_inline_nvi1i3oqvu1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: In the film, Astronaut Mark Watney is stranded on the Red Planet. </p>\n<p>REALITY: In preparation for sending humans to Mars, we have completed one of the most extensive isolation missions in Hawaii, known as <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/feature/hi-seas-team-completes-8-month-isolation-mission\">HI-SEAS</a>. The goal of this study was to see how isolation and the lack of privacy in a small group affects social aspects of would-be explorers. The most recent simulation was eight months long, and the next mission is planned to last a year.</p>\n<p><b>Spaceport</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1041\" data-orig-height=\"521\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/3fd1b83871ac9e2c90c431dbde4ff475/tumblr_inline_nvi1jz3GbG1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1041\" data-orig-height=\"521\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: The Martian movie launches astronauts on the Aries missions from a refurbished and state of the art space center. </p>\n<p>REALITY: Currently, the <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/systems/ground/index.html\">Ground Systems Development and Operations’</a> primary objective is to prepare the center to process and launch the next-generation vehicles and spacecraft designed to achieve our goals for space exploration. We are not only working to develop new systems, but also refurbishing and upgrading infrastructure to meet future demands. </p>\n<p><b>Deep Space Propulsion </b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://41.media.tumblr.com/329c0d27f8782953ead30eb1e5c1d0f1/tumblr_inline_nvi1ktILTr1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: In the film, the astronauts depart the Red Planet using a propulsion system know as the Mars Ascent Vehicle (MAV). </p>\n<p>REALITY: We are currently developing the most powerful rocket we’ve ever built, our <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/systems/sls/index.html\">Space Launch System</a> (SLS). Once complete, this system will enable astronauts to travel deeper into the solar system than ever before! The <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/sls/brain-for-rs-25-engine.html\">RS-25 engines</a> that will be used on the SLS, were previously utilized as the main engine on our space shuttles. These engines have proven their reliability and are currently being refurbished with updated and improved technology for our journey to Mars.</p>\n<p><b>Mission Control</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/5d26ae2356623b92a1090a5f383251e4/tumblr_inline_nvi1lbsmLs1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: In the movie, Mission Control operations support the Aries 3 crew. </p>\n<p>REALITY: On our real journey to Mars, <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/press-release/mission-control-houston-marks-50th-birthday-with-look-back-look-ahead\">Mission Control</a> in Houston will support our Orion spacecraft and the crew onboard as they travel into deep space. </p>\n<p><b>Habitat</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/e9393fb9ab96f0875f1d873efa7ef64c/tumblr_inline_nvi1ls7fxm1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: The artificial living habitat on Mars in The Martian movie is constructed of industrial canvas and contains an array of life support systems. </p>\n<p>REALITY: The <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/hrp/research/analogs/hera\">Human Exploration Research Analog (HERA)</a>, formerly known as the <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/technology/deep_space_habitat/\">Deep Space Habitat</a>, is a three-story module that was designed and created through a series of university competitions. Studies conducted in habitat mockups will allow us to evolve this technology to create a reliable structures for use on Mars.</p>\n<p><b>Rover</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/cfc01537f1e0044553d9ca1464c50d27/tumblr_inline_nvi1m7W9cl1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: The characters in the film are able to cruise around the Red Planet inside the Mars Decent Vehicle (MDV). </p>\n<p>REALITY: We are currently developing a next generation vehicle for space exploration. Our <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/pdf/541196main_Analogs_FactSheet_508.pdf\">Mars Exploration Vehicle</a> <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/technology/space_exploration_vehicle/index.html\">(MEV)</a> is designed to be flexible depending on the destination. It will have a pressurized cabin, ability to house two astronauts for up to 14 days and will be about the size of a pickup truck. </p>\n<p><b>Harvest</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/b7d11a79000b8beb10b0e8a133cf15a6/tumblr_inline_nvi1mnlhp61tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: Astronaut Mark Watney grows potatoes on Mars in The Martian movie. </p>\n<p>REALITY: We’re already growing and <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/mission_pages/station/research/news/meals_ready_to_eat\">harvesting lettuce</a> on the International Space Station in preparation for deep space exploration. Growing fresh food in space will provide future pioneers with a sustainable food supplement, and could also be used for recreational gardening during deep space missions. </p>\n<p><b>Spacesuit</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/33f6e7349577339b2f015d65c96f58ee/tumblr_inline_nvi1n85xZE1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: The spacesuit worn by astronauts in the film allows them to work and function on the surface of Mars, while protecting them from the harsh environment.</p>\n<p>REALITY: Prototypes of our <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/suitup\">Z-2 Exploration Suit</a> are helping to develop the technologies astronauts will use to live and work on the the Martian surface. Technology advances in this <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/technology/advanced_space_suits/index.html#.VgwSMRNVhHw\">next generation spacesuit</a> would shorten preparation time, improve safety and boost astronaut capabilities during spacewalks and surface activities.  </p>\n</blockquote>",

            "content_raw": "<p>The Martian movie is set 20 years in the future, but here at NASA we are already developing many of the technologies that appear in the film. The movie takes the work we’re doing and extends it into fiction set in the 2030s, when NASA astronauts are regularly traveling to Mars and living on the surface. Here are a few ways The Martian movie compares to what we’re really doing on our journey to Mars:</p>\n<p><b>Analog Missions</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/b93f3d9373c5fe5ccdfbd79e7c0d472e/tumblr_inline_nvi1i3oqvu1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"></figure><p>MOVIE: In the film, Astronaut Mark Watney is stranded on the Red Planet. </p>\n<p>REALITY: In preparation for sending humans to Mars, we have completed one of the most extensive isolation missions in Hawaii, known as <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/feature/hi-seas-team-completes-8-month-isolation-mission\">HI-SEAS</a>. The goal of this study was to see how isolation and the lack of privacy in a small group affects social aspects of would-be explorers. The most recent simulation was eight months long, and the next mission is planned to last a year.</p>\n<p><b>Spaceport</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1041\" data-orig-height=\"521\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/3fd1b83871ac9e2c90c431dbde4ff475/tumblr_inline_nvi1jz3GbG1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1041\" data-orig-height=\"521\"></figure><p>MOVIE: The Martian movie launches astronauts on the Aries missions from a refurbished and state of the art space center. </p>\n<p>REALITY: Currently, the <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/systems/ground/index.html\">Ground Systems Development and Operations’</a> primary objective is to prepare the center to process and launch the next-generation vehicles and spacecraft designed to achieve our goals for space exploration. We are not only working to develop new systems, but also refurbishing and upgrading infrastructure to meet future demands. </p>\n<p><b>Deep Space Propulsion </b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://41.media.tumblr.com/329c0d27f8782953ead30eb1e5c1d0f1/tumblr_inline_nvi1ktILTr1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"></figure><p>MOVIE: In the film, the astronauts depart the Red Planet using a propulsion system know as the Mars Ascent Vehicle (MAV). </p>\n<p>REALITY: We are currently developing the most powerful rocket we’ve ever built, our <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/systems/sls/index.html\">Space Launch System</a> (SLS). Once complete, this system will enable astronauts to travel deeper into the solar system than ever before! The <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/sls/brain-for-rs-25-engine.html\">RS-25 engines</a> that will be used on the SLS, were previously utilized as the main engine on our space shuttles. These engines have proven their reliability and are currently being refurbished with updated and improved technology for our journey to Mars.</p>\n<p><b>Mission Control</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/5d26ae2356623b92a1090a5f383251e4/tumblr_inline_nvi1lbsmLs1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"></figure><p>MOVIE: In the movie, Mission Control operations support the Aries 3 crew. </p>\n<p>REALITY: On our real journey to Mars, <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/press-release/mission-control-houston-marks-50th-birthday-with-look-back-look-ahead\">Mission Control</a> in Houston will support our Orion spacecraft and the crew onboard as they travel into deep space. </p>\n<p><b>Habitat</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/e9393fb9ab96f0875f1d873efa7ef64c/tumblr_inline_nvi1ls7fxm1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"></figure><p>MOVIE: The artificial living habitat on Mars in The Martian movie is constructed of industrial canvas and contains an array of life support systems. </p>\n<p>REALITY: The <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/hrp/research/analogs/hera\">Human Exploration Research Analog (HERA)</a>, formerly known as the <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/technology/deep_space_habitat/\">Deep Space Habitat</a>, is a three-story module that was designed and created through a series of university competitions. Studies conducted in habitat mockups will allow us to evolve this technology to create a reliable structures for use on Mars.</p>\n<p><b>Rover</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/cfc01537f1e0044553d9ca1464c50d27/tumblr_inline_nvi1m7W9cl1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"></figure><p>MOVIE: The characters in the film are able to cruise around the Red Planet inside the Mars Decent Vehicle (MDV). </p>\n<p>REALITY: We are currently developing a next generation vehicle for space exploration. Our <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/pdf/541196main_Analogs_FactSheet_508.pdf\">Mars Exploration Vehicle</a> <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/technology/space_exploration_vehicle/index.html\">(MEV)</a> is designed to be flexible depending on the destination. It will have a pressurized cabin, ability to house two astronauts for up to 14 days and will be about the size of a pickup truck. </p>\n<p><b>Harvest</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/b7d11a79000b8beb10b0e8a133cf15a6/tumblr_inline_nvi1mnlhp61tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"></figure><p>MOVIE: Astronaut Mark Watney grows potatoes on Mars in The Martian movie. </p>\n<p>REALITY: We’re already growing and <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/mission_pages/station/research/news/meals_ready_to_eat\">harvesting lettuce</a> on the International Space Station in preparation for deep space exploration. Growing fresh food in space will provide future pioneers with a sustainable food supplement, and could also be used for recreational gardening during deep space missions. </p>\n<p><b>Spacesuit</b></p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/33f6e7349577339b2f015d65c96f58ee/tumblr_inline_nvi1n85xZE1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1280\" data-orig-height=\"720\"></figure><p>MOVIE: The spacesuit worn by astronauts in the film allows them to work and function on the surface of Mars, while protecting them from the harsh environment.</p>\n<p>REALITY: Prototypes of our <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/suitup\">Z-2 Exploration Suit</a> are helping to develop the technologies astronauts will use to live and work on the the Martian surface. Technology advances in this <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/exploration/technology/advanced_space_suits/index.html#.VgwSMRNVhHw\">next generation spacesuit</a> would shorten preparation time, improve safety and boost astronaut capabilities during spacewalks and surface activities.  </p>",
            "content": "<p>The Martian movie is set 20 years in the future, but here at NASA we are already developing many of the technologies that appear in the film. The movie takes the work we’re doing and extends it into fiction set in the 2030s, when NASA astronauts are regularly traveling to Mars and living on the surface. Here are a few ways The Martian movie compares to what we’re really doing on our journey to Mars:</p>\n<p><b>Analog Missions</b></p>\n<figure class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/b93f3d9373c5fe5ccdfbd79e7c0d472e/tumblr_inline_nvi1i3oqvu1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" class=\"\"/></figure><p>MOVIE: In the film, Astronaut Mark Watney is stranded on the Red Planet. </p>\n<p>REALITY: In preparation for sending humans to Mars, we have completed one of the most extensive isolation missions in Hawaii, known as <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/feature/hi-seas-team-completes-8-month-isolation-mission\">HI-SEAS</a>. The goal of this study was to see how isolation and the lack of privacy in a small group affects social aspects of would-be explorers.         "title": "Water on Mars!",
        "body": "<p><a class=\"tumblr_blog\" href=\"http://nasa.tumblr.com/post/130083388029\">nasa</a>:</p>\n<blockquote>\n<p><figure data-orig-width=\"1650\" data-orig-height=\"857\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/a63efb94cf645bc13acd5fe89a89bf47/tumblr_inline_nvek27v7oB1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1650\" data-orig-height=\"857\"/></figure></p><p>Did you hear? New findings from our <a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/mission_pages/MRO/main/\">Mars Reconnaissance Orbiter (MRO)</a> provide the strongest evidence yet that <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/press-release/nasa-confirms-evidence-that-liquid-water-flows-on-today-s-mars\">liquid water flows</a> intermittently on present-day Mars. </p>\n<p>Using an imaging spectrometer on MRO, we found hydrated minerals on slopes where <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/image-feature/jpl/pia19916/recurring-lineae-on-slopes-at-hale-crater-mars\">mysterious streaks</a> are seen on Mars. One thing that researchers noticed was that the darkish streaks appear to ebb and flow over time. During warm seasons, they darken and then fade in cooler seasons. </p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1374\" data-orig-height=\"714\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/8f50e585a92ab18af05a5908b3482f56/tumblr_inline_nvek14cAvS1tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1374\" data-orig-height=\"714\"/></figure><p>When discovered in 2010, these downhill flows known as <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/image-feature/jpl/pia19917/dark-recurring-streaks-on-walls-of-garni-crater\">recurring slope lineae (RSL)</a> were thought to be related to liquid water. With the recent spectral detection of molecular water, we’re able to say it’s likely a shallow subsurface flow explains the darkening. </p>\n<p><b>Mars is so cold, how could liquid water flow there?</b> Great question! Since this liquid water is briny, the freezing point would be lower than that of pure water. Also, these saline slopes appear on Mars when temperatures are above minus 10 degrees Fahrenheit (minus 23 Celsius). </p>\n<p>The <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/image-feature/jpl/pia19918/recurring-lineae-on-slopes-at-horowitz-crater\">dark, narrow streaks</a> flowing downhill in the below image are roughly the length of a football field. </p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"1920\" data-orig-height=\"997\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/513fcad16e8885022c1fd600683edc37/tumblr_inline_nvek0vstW61tzhl5u_540.jpg\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"1920\" data-orig-height=\"997\"/></figure><p><b>So there’s water, but how much? </b>Currently we think this area has a very small amount of water, probably just enough to wet the top layer of the surface of Mars. The streaks are around four to five meters wide and 200 to 300 meters long. </p>\n<p><b>Could humans drink this water?</b> The salts in the water appear to be perchlorates, so you probably wouldn’t want to drink the water. It would most likely be very salty and would need to be purified before human consumption. </p>\n<p><b>Perchlorate…What is that? </b>A perchlorate is a salt that absorbs water from the air. Learn more about how it’s helping us unlock the mysteries of Mars in this video:</p>\n<figure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\" data-provider=\"youtube\" data-orig-width=\"540\" data-orig-height=\"304\" data-url=\"https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DfxnEKi7ItW4\"><iframe width=\"540\" height=\"304\" id=\"youtube_iframe\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/fxnEKi7ItW4?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://safe.txmblr.com&amp;wmode=opaque\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></figure><p><b>What’s next? </b>We want to look for more locations where brine flows may occur. We have only covered 3% of Mars at resolutions high enough to see these features.</p>\n<p>For more information on the Mars announcement, visit our <a href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/topics/journeytomars/index.html\">Journey to Mars</a> landing page. There is also a full recap of the press conference <a href=\"https://youtu.be/MRQ5B_ik2dU\">HERE</a>, and a short recap below. </p>\n<figure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\" data-provider=\"youtube\" data-orig-width=\"540\" data-orig-height=\"304\" data-url=\"https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DbDv4FRHI3J8\"><iframe width=\"540\" height=\"304\" id=\"youtube_iframe\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/bDv4FRHI3J8?feature=oembed&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https://safe.txmblr.com&amp;wmode=opaque\" frameborder=\"0\"></iframe></figure><p><i>Make sure to follow us on Tumblr for your regular dose of space: </i><a href=\"http://nasa.tumblr.com/\"><i><a href=\"http://nasa.tumblr.com\">http://nasa.tumblr.com</a></i></a></p>\n</blockquote>",

There are usually 4 to 6 supermoons every year. </p>\n<p>Observers can view the total eclipse on September 27, starting at 10:11 p.m. EDT until 11:23 p.m. This event will be visible in North and South America, as well as Europe and Africa. Uranus and Neptune at midnight, and Venus, Mars and Jupiter in the pre-dawn sky. </p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"400\" data-orig-height=\"225\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://33.media.tumblr.com/e6abfe561e9295868af5b6fe1b862f70/tumblr_inline_nu22seCEz91tzhl5u_500.gif\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"400\" data-orig-height=\"225\"></figure><p>Finally, if you’re able to escape to a dark location, you might be able to see a great view of our Milky Way! </p>\n<p>So, make sure to get outside this month and take a look at everything our night sky has to offer. </p>\n<figure data-orig-width=\"400\" data-orig-height=\"225\" class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://38.media.tumblr.com/1470238b177ddda26b8c1ea7459d7f91/tumblr_inline_nu2305Tcq91tzhl5u_500.gif\" alt=\"image\" data-orig-width=\"400\" data-orig-height=\"225\"></figure><p><i>Make sure to follow us on Tumblr for your regular dose of space: <a href=\"http://nasa.tumblr.com/\">http://nasa.tumblr.com</a> </i><br></p>",
            "content": "<p><figure class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://38.media.tumblr.com/57938372f6b853f2649f04e7486d8303/tumblr_inline_nu222xNp7J1tzhl5u_500.gif\" class=\"\"/></figure>\n<p>Stargazing and looking up into the night sky is always a fun thing to do. <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jXMZmEOGLRc\">This month</a>, it will be especially exciting because there will be a total eclipse of a supermoon, plus the opportunity to see planets and the late-summer Milky Way!</p>\n<p><b>What is a supermoon? </b></p>\n<figure class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://38.media.tumblr.com/0c5c8d915284bf08d350468b3e8b9aad/tumblr_inline_nu22c5MP901tzhl5u_500.gif\" class=\"\"/></figure><p>A supermoon is a new or full moon that occurs when it is at, or near its closest approach to Earth in a given orbit. There are usually 4 to 6 supermoons every year. </p>\n<p>Observers can view the total eclipse on September 27, starting at 10:11 p.m. EDT until 11:23 p.m. This event will be visible in North and South America, as well as Europe and Africa. So make sure to mark your calendars! </p>\n<figure class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://40.media.tumblr.com/0e54db10414bc902bf8e29b5cda0681a/tumblr_inline_nu22lkFW4J1tzhl5u_540.png\" class=\"\"/></figure><p>This month, you will also be able to see the planets! Look for Mercury, Saturn, Pluto and Neptune in the evening sky. Uranus and Neptune at midnight, and Venus, Mars and Jupiter in the pre-dawn sky. </p>\n<figure class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://33.media.tumblr.com/e6abfe561e9295868af5b6fe1b862f70/tumblr_inline_nu22seCEz91tzhl5u_500.gif\" class=\"\"/></figure><p>Finally, if you’re able to escape to a dark location, you might be able to see a great view of our Milky Way! </p>\n<p>So, make sure to get outside this month and take a look at everything our night sky has to offer. </p>\n<figure class=\"tmblr-full\"><img src=\"http://38.media.tumblr.com/1470238b177ddda26b8c1ea7459d7f91/tumblr_inline_nu2305Tcq91tzhl5u_500.gif\" class=\"\"/></figure><p><i>Make sure to follow us on Tumblr for your regular dose of space: <a href=\"http://nasa.tumblr.com/\">http://nasa.tumblr.com</a> </i><br /></p></p>",
